# Changelog

## [v2026.05.09](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/tree/v2026.05.09) (2026-05-09)

[Full Changelog](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/compare/v2024.01.21...v2026.05.09)

**Fixed bugs:**

- script.py without "\(" print command [\#3068](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/3068)
- Mock assertion issue with ICU recipe under Python 3.12 [\#3002](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/3002)
- sympy recipe build fail [\#2820](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2820)
- libzmq recipy build fail [\#2811](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2811)
- libmysqlclient recipe build fail [\#2808](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2808)
- greenlet recipe build fail [\#2806](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2806)
- gevent recipe build fail [\#2805](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2805)
- atom recipe build fail [\#2802](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2802)
- dlopen failed: cannot locate symbol "\_ZNSt12length\_errorD1Ev" while loading matplotlib/\_path.so on Android 12 [\#2675](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2675)
- Changing android.arch or android.api does not trigger the appropriate re-build. [\#1917](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/1917)
- TypeError: must be str, not bytes  [\#1885](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/1885)
- PythonActivity.java is calling considerLoadingScreenRemoval too early [\#1884](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/1884)
- apk build error: libtinfo.so.5: cannot open shared object file: No such file or directory [\#1858](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/1858)
- fix for non standard path for libraries. [\#1261](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/1261)

## [v2024.01.21](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/tree/v2024.01.21) (2024-01-23)

[Full Changelog](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/compare/v2023.09.16...v2024.01.21)

**Fixed bugs:**

- Update documentation copyright [\#2921](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2921)
- Support mail address is broken [\#2899](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2899)
- doc/macos/jdk: invalid brew install command provided. [\#2896](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2896)
- pyzmq recipe build fail [\#2818](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/2818)

- python3 + openssl compilation fail [\#1590](https://github.com/kivy/python-for-android/issues/1590)
